        .               /// Walks upwards from `id` to find a node which might change lint levels with attributes.
        .               /// It stops at `bound` and just returns it if reached.
  619,640 ( 0.00%)      pub fn maybe_lint_level_root_bounded(self, mut id: HirId, bound: HirId) -> HirId {
  619,640 ( 0.00%)          let hir = self.hir();
        .                   loop {

        .                           return bound;
        .                       }
        .

        .                           return id;
